--// SERVICES
local Players = game:GetService("Players")
local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
local Workspace = game:GetService("Workspace")
local RunService = game:GetService("RunService")

--// LOCAL PLAYER & CHARACTER
local plr = Players.LocalPlayer
local character = plr.Character or plr.CharacterAdded:Wait()
local humanoid = character:WaitForChild("Humanoid")

--// UPDATE CHARACTER WHEN RESPAWNED
plr.CharacterAdded:Connect(function(char)
    character = char
    humanoid = char:WaitForChild("Humanoid")
end)

--=============================================================================
-- SPECTRA HUB LIBRARY (UI)
--=============================================================================

    Title = "Spectra hub",
    SubTitle = "by: assure_TV versão 20.2",
    Icon = "rbxassetid://111496334196615",                -- ícone opcional

    BackgroundImageTransparency = 0,                      -- transparência
    SaveFolder = "spectra hub"
})

    Size = UDim2.fromOffset(50, 50),
    Button = { Image = "rbxassetid://72497169270723", BackgroundTransparency = 0 },
    Corner = { CornerRadius = UDim.new(0.5, 0) }         -- círculo perfeito
})

--===============================
-- DETECTOR DE EXECUTOR
--===============================
local function detectExecutor()
    if identifyexecutor then
        return identifyexecutor()
    elseif syn then
        return "Synapse X"
    elseif KRNL_LOADED then
        return "KRNL"
    elseif is_sirhurt_closure then
        return "SirHurt"
    elseif pebc_execute then
        return "ProtoSmasher"
    elseif getexecutorname then
        return getexecutorname()
    else
        return "Executor Desconhecido"
    end
end

local executorName = detectExecutor()

Tab1:AddParagraph({
    "Executor",
    executorName
})

Tab1:AddParagraph({
    "Jogador",
    game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.Name
})


--===============================
-- SEÇÃO: CRIADORES

})

})

--=============================================================================
-- TAB: LOCAL PLAYER
--=============================================================================
local LocalTab = Window:MakeTab({
    Title = "Player",
    Icon = "rbxassetid://7733765398"
})

--=============================================================================
-- STATUS
--=============================================================================
LocalTab:AddSection({"Status do Player"})

-- SPEED
LocalTab:AddSlider({
    Name = "Velocidade",
    Min = 1,
    Max = 2000,
    Default = 16,
    Callback = function(Value)
        if humanoid then
            humanoid.WalkSpeed = Value
        end
    end
})

-- JUMP
LocalTab:AddSlider({
    Name = "Força do Pulo",
    Min = 1,
    Max = 2000,
    Default = 50,
    Callback = function(Value)
        if humanoid then
            humanoid.JumpPower = Value
        end
    end
})

-- GRAVIDADE
LocalTab:AddSlider({
    Name = "Gravidade",
    Min = 1,
    Max = 2000,
    Default = 196,
    Callback = function(Value)
        Workspace.Gravity = Value
    end
})

-- RESET
LocalTab:AddButton({
    Name = "Resetar Status",
    Callback = function()
        if humanoid then
            humanoid.WalkSpeed = 16
            humanoid.JumpPower = 50
        end
        Workspace.Gravity = 196
    end
})

--=============================================================================
-- MOVIMENTO
--=============================================================================
LocalTab:AddSection({"Movimento"})

-- INFINITY JUMP
local infJump = false

LocalTab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Infinity Jump",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(v)
        infJump = v
    end
})

game:GetService("UserInputService").JumpRequest:Connect(function()
    if infJump and humanoid then
        humanoid:ChangeState(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Jumping)
    end
end)

-- NOCLIP
local noclip = false

LocalTab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Noclip",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(v)
        noclip = v
    end
})

RunService.Stepped:Connect(function()
    if noclip and character then
        for _,v in pairs(character:GetDescendants()) do
            if v:IsA("BasePart") then
                v.CanCollide = false
            end
        end
    end
end)

--=============================================================================
-- SPIN
--=============================================================================
LocalTab:AddSection({"Spin"})

local spin = false
local spinSpeed = 50

LocalTab:AddSlider({
    Name = "Velocidade Spin",
    Min = 1,
    Max = 5000,
    Default = 50,
    Callback = function(v)
        spinSpeed = v
    end
})

LocalTab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Spin",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(v)
        spin = v
    end
})

RunService.RenderStepped:Connect(function()
    if spin and character and character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
        character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame =
        character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame *
        CFrame.Angles(0, math.rad(spinSpeed), 0)
    end
end)





-- ===============================
-- ESP
-- ===============================
LocalTab:AddSection({ "ESP" })

_G.ESPData = {
    espEnabled = false,
    espType = "Nome + Idade",
    selectedColor = "RGB",
    billboardGuis = {},
    highlights = {},
    lines = {},
    connections = {}
}

local Players = game:GetService("Players")
local RunService = game:GetService("RunService")
local Camera = workspace.CurrentCamera

-- ===============================
-- COR
-- ===============================
local function getESPColor()

    if _G.ESPData.selectedColor == "RGB" then
        local h = (tick() % 5) / 5
        return Color3.fromHSV(h,1,1)
    end

    local colors = {
        Branco = Color3.fromRGB(255,255,255),
        Preto = Color3.fromRGB(0,0,0),
        Vermelho = Color3.fromRGB(255,0,0),
        Verde = Color3.fromRGB(0,255,0),
        Azul = Color3.fromRGB(0,170,255),
        Amarelo = Color3.fromRGB(255,255,0),
        Rosa = Color3.fromRGB(255,105,180),
        Roxo = Color3.fromRGB(128,0,128)
    }

    return colors[_G.ESPData.selectedColor] or Color3.new(1,1,1)

end

-- ===============================
-- LIMPAR ESP
-- ===============================
_G.clearAllESP = function()

    for _,v in pairs(_G.ESPData.billboardGuis) do
        pcall(function() v:Destroy() end)
    end

    for _,v in pairs(_G.ESPData.highlights) do
        pcall(function() v:Destroy() end)
    end

    for _,v in pairs(_G.ESPData.lines) do
        pcall(function() v:Remove() end)
    end

    for _,v in pairs(_G.ESPData.connections) do
        pcall(function() v:Disconnect() end)
    end

    _G.ESPData.billboardGuis = {}
    _G.ESPData.highlights = {}
    _G.ESPData.lines = {}
    _G.ESPData.connections = {}

end

-- ===============================
-- NAME ESP
-- ===============================
local function createNameESP(player)

    if player == Players.LocalPlayer then return end
    if not player.Character then return end
    if not player.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") then return end

    local gui = Instance.new("BillboardGui")
    gui.Size = UDim2.new(0,200,0,50)
    gui.StudsOffset = Vector3.new(0,3,0)
    gui.AlwaysOnTop = true
    gui.Parent = player.Character.Head

    local txt = Instance.new("TextLabel")
    txt.Size = UDim2.new(1,0,1,0)
    txt.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    txt.TextStrokeTransparency = 0.5
    txt.Font = Enum.Font.SourceSansBold
    txt.TextSize = 14
    txt.Text = player.Name.." | "..player.AccountAge.." dias"
    txt.TextColor3 = getESPColor()
    txt.Parent = gui

    _G.ESPData.billboardGuis[player] = gui

end

-- ===============================
-- HIGHLIGHT ESP
-- ===============================
local function createHighlightESP(player)

    if player == Players.LocalPlayer then return end
    if not player.Character then return end

    local h = Instance.new("Highlight")
    h.FillColor = getESPColor()
    h.FillTransparency = 0.5
    h.OutlineTransparency = 0
    h.DepthMode = Enum.HighlightDepthMode.AlwaysOnTop
    h.Parent = player.Character

    _G.ESPData.highlights[player] = h

end

-- ===============================
-- LINE ESP
-- ===============================
local function createLineESP(player)

    if player == Players.LocalPlayer then return end

    local line = Drawing.new("Line")
    line.Thickness = 2
    line.Transparency = 1
    line.Visible = false

    _G.ESPData.lines[player] = line

end

-- ===============================
-- APPLY ESP
-- ===============================
_G.applyCurrentESP = function()

    _G.clearAllESP()

    if not _G.ESPData.espEnabled then return end

    for _,p in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do

        if _G.ESPData.espType == "Nome + Idade" then
            createNameESP(p)

        elseif _G.ESPData.espType == "Corpo (Highlight)" then
            createHighlightESP(p)

        elseif _G.ESPData.espType == "Linhas" then
            createLineESP(p)
        end

    end

    table.insert(_G.ESPData.connections,

        RunService.RenderStepped:Connect(function()

            if not _G.ESPData.espEnabled then return end

            local color = getESPColor()

            if _G.ESPData.espType == "Linhas" then

                for p,line in pairs(_G.ESPData.lines) do

                    if p.Character and p.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then

                        local pos,onScreen =
                        Camera:WorldToViewportPoint(p.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position)

                        line.Visible = onScreen

                        if onScreen then
                            line.From = Vector2.new(Camera.ViewportSize.X/2,Camera.ViewportSize.Y)
                            line.To = Vector2.new(pos.X,pos.Y)
                            line.Color = color
                        end

                    else
                        line.Visible = false
                    end

                end

            end

        end)

    )

end

-- ===============================
-- UI
-- ===============================

LocalTab:AddDropdown({
    Name = "Tipo de ESP",
    Options = {"Nome + Idade","Corpo (Highlight)","Linhas"},
    Default = 1,
    Callback = function(v)

        _G.ESPData.espType = v

        if _G.ESPData.espEnabled then
            _G.applyCurrentESP()
        end

    end
})

LocalTab:AddDropdown({
    Name = "Cor do ESP",
    Options = {"RGB","Branco","Preto","Vermelho","Verde","Azul","Amarelo","Rosa","Roxo"},
    Default = 1,
    Callback = function(v)

        _G.ESPData.selectedColor = v

    end
})

LocalTab:AddToggle({
    Name = "ESP Ativado",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(v)

        _G.ESPData.espEnabled = v

        if v then
            _G.applyCurrentESP()
        else
            _G.clearAllESP()
        end

    end
})


--=============================================================================
-- TAB CASA
--=============================================================================
local Tab4 = Window:MakeTab({
    Title = "Casa",
    Icon = "rbxassetid://8301879545"
})

--=============================================================================
-- PARÁGRAFO
--=============================================================================
Tab4:AddParagraph({
    Title = "Funções para você usar em você",
    Content = ""
})

--=============================================================================
-- REMOVER BAN DAS CASAS
--=============================================================================
Tab4:AddButton({
    Name = "Remover Ban de Todas as Casas",
    Description = "Tenta remover o ban de todas as casas",
    Callback = function()

        local successCount = 0
        local failCount = 0

        for i = 1,37 do
            local bannedBlockName = "BannedBlock"..i
            local bannedBlock = workspace:FindFirstChild(bannedBlockName,true)

            if bannedBlock then
                local success = pcall(function()
                    bannedBlock:Destroy()
                end)

                if success then
                    successCount = successCount + 1
                else
                    failCount = failCount + 1
                end
            end
        end

        for _,house in pairs(workspace:GetDescendants()) do
            if house.Name:match("BannedBlock") then

                local success = pcall(function()
                    house:Destroy()
                end)

                if success then
                    successCount = successCount + 1
                else
                    failCount = failCount + 1
                end

            end
        end

        if successCount > 0 then
            game.StarterGui:SetCore("SendNotification",{
                Title = "Sucesso",
                Text = "Bans removidos de "..successCount.." casas!",
                Duration = 5
            })
        end

        if failCount > 0 then
            game.StarterGui:SetCore("SendNotification",{
                Title = "Aviso",
                Text = "Falha ao remover bans de "..failCount.." casas.",
                Duration = 5
            })
        end

        if successCount == 0 and failCount == 0 then
            game.StarterGui:SetCore("SendNotification",{
                Title = "Aviso",
                Text = "Nenhum ban encontrado para remover.",
                Duration = 5
            })
        end

    end
})

--=============================================================================
-- RGB CASA
--=============================================================================
Tab4:AddSection({"RGB Casa"})

local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")

local rgbSpeed = 3
local rgbCasa = false

-- SLIDER VELOCIDADE
Tab4:AddSlider({
    Name = "Velocidade RGB",
    Min = 1,
    Max = 26,
    Default = 3,
    Callback = function(v)
        rgbSpeed = v
    end
})

-- FUNÇÃO COR RGB
local function getRainbowColor(speed)

    local h = (tick() * speed % 10) / 10
    return Color3.fromHSV(h,1,1)

end

-- FUNÇÃO REMOTE
local function fireServer(eventName,args)

    local RE = ReplicatedStorage:FindFirstChild("RE")

    if RE and RE:FindFirstChild(eventName) then
        pcall(function()
            RE[eventName]:FireServer(unpack(args))
        end)
    end

end

-- TOGGLE RGB CASA
Tab4:AddToggle({
    Name = "RGB Casa",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(state)

        rgbCasa = state

        if state then

            task.spawn(function()

                while rgbCasa do

                    fireServer("1Player1sHous1e",{
                        "ColorPickHouse",
                        getRainbowColor(rgbSpeed)
                    })

                    task.wait(0.1)

                end

            end)

        end

    end
})

--=============================================================================
-- PARÁGRAFO FINAL
--=============================================================================
Tab4:AddParagraph({
    Title = "por em quanto so isso :p",
    Content = ""
})







--////////////////////////////////////////////////////
--// TROLL TAB
local TrollTab = Window:MakeTab({
    Title = "Troll",
    Icon = "rbxassetid://7734058599"
})

--////////////////////////////////////////////////////
--// PLAYER LIST
local selectedPlayer

local function getPlayers()
    local t = {}

    for _, p in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
        if p ~= plr then
            table.insert(t, p.Name)
        end
    end

    return t
end

local dropdown = TrollTab:AddDropdown({
    Name = "Escolher Player",
    Options = getPlayers(),
    Callback = function(v)
        selectedPlayer = v
    end
})

TrollTab:AddButton({
    Name = "Atualizar Lista",
    Callback = function()
        dropdown:Set(getPlayers())
    end
})

--====================================================
-- SPECTATE
--====================================================
local RunService = game:GetService("RunService")
local Camera = workspace.CurrentCamera
local LocalPlayer = Players.LocalPlayer

local spectating = false
local spectateConn
local charConn
local currentTarget

-- RESET CAMERA
local function resetCamera()

    if spectateConn then
        spectateConn:Disconnect()
        spectateConn = nil
    end

    if charConn then
        charConn:Disconnect()
        charConn = nil
    end

    currentTarget = nil

    local char = LocalPlayer.Character
    local hum = char and char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")

    if hum then
        Camera.CameraSubject = hum
        Camera.CameraType = Enum.CameraType.Custom
    end

end

-- SPECTAR PLAYER
local function spectatePlayer(player)

    if not spectating or not player then return end

    resetCamera()

    spectating = true
    currentTarget = player

    spectateConn = RunService.RenderStepped:Connect(function()

        if not spectating then return end
        if not currentTarget or not currentTarget.Character then return end

        local hum = currentTarget.Character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")

        if hum then
            Camera.CameraSubject = hum
            Camera.CameraType = Enum.CameraType.Custom
        end

    end)

    charConn = player.CharacterAdded:Connect(function()
        task.wait(0.1)

        if spectating and currentTarget == player then
            spectatePlayer(player)
        end
    end)

end

-- PLAYER SAINDO
Players.PlayerRemoving:Connect(function(player)

    if spectating and currentTarget == player then
        resetCamera()
        spectating = false
    end

end)

--====================================================
-- TOGGLE SPECTATE
--====================================================
TrollTab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Spectar Jogador",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(state)

        spectating = state

        if not state then
            resetCamera()
            return
        end

        local target = Players:FindFirstChild(selectedPlayer)

        if target then
            spectatePlayer(target)
        else
            resetCamera()
        end

    end
})

--====================================================
-- TROCAR PLAYER SEM QUEBRAR
--====================================================
task.spawn(function()

    local lastSelected

    while true do
        task.wait(0.15)

        if not spectating then
            lastSelected = nil
            continue
        end

        if selectedPlayer ~= lastSelected then

            lastSelected = selectedPlayer

            local newTarget = Players:FindFirstChild(selectedPlayer)

            if newTarget then
                spectatePlayer(newTarget)
            else
                resetCamera()
            end

        end
    end

end)

--====================================================
-- TELEPORTAR PARA PLAYER
--====================================================
TrollTab:AddButton({
    Name = "Teleportar no Jogador",
    Callback = function()

        if not selectedPlayer then return end

        local target = Players:FindFirstChild(selectedPlayer)
        if not target or not target.Character then return end

        local myChar = plr.Character
        local myHRP = myChar and myChar:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
        local targetHRP = target.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")

        if myHRP and targetHRP then
            myHRP.CFrame = targetHRP.CFrame * CFrame.new(0,0,-3)
        end

    end
})


TrollTab:AddSection({"killS"})


local running = false
local seated = false
local sitConn

-- RESET QUANDO MORRER
plr.CharacterAdded:Connect(function()
    running = false
    seated = false

    if sitConn then
        sitConn:Disconnect()
        sitConn = nil
    end
end)

TrollTab:AddButton({
    Name = "KILL",
    Callback = function()

        if running or not selectedPlayer then return end

        local character = plr.Character
        if not character then return end

        local humanoid = character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
        local hrp = character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
        if not humanoid or not hrp then return end

        local target = Players:FindFirstChild(selectedPlayer)
        if not target or not target.Character then return end

        local targetHumanoid = target.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
        local targetHRP = target.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
        if not targetHumanoid or not targetHRP then return end

        running = true
        seated = false

        -- BODY SIZE
        for i = 1,12 do
            ReplicatedStorage.Remotes.IncrementBodySize:FireServer(false)
        end

        -- PEGAR COUCH
        local hasCouch = false

        if character:FindFirstChild("Couch") then
            hasCouch = true
        end

        for _,tool in ipairs(plr.Backpack:GetChildren()) do
            if tool.Name == "Couch" then
                hasCouch = true
            end
        end

        if not hasCouch then
            ReplicatedStorage.RE["1Too1l"]:InvokeServer("PickingTools","Couch")
            task.wait(0.3)
        end

        local couch = plr.Backpack:FindFirstChild("Couch")
        if couch then
            humanoid:EquipTool(couch)
        end

        task.wait(0.2)

        hrp.CFrame = targetHRP.CFrame * CFrame.new(0,0,-2)

        if sitConn then
            sitConn:Disconnect()
        end

        sitConn = targetHumanoid.Seated:Connect(function(active)

            if active then
                seated = true
                running = false

                sitConn:Disconnect()

                hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(-54.24,-298.21,-184.12)

                task.wait(0.3)

                humanoid:UnequipTools()

                task.wait(0.7)

                hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(-27.59,4.27,-16.84)
            end

        end)

        task.spawn(function()

            local tickSide = 1

            while running and not seated do

                local base = targetHRP.Position

                local offsets = {

                    Vector3.new(3 * tickSide,0,0),
                    Vector3.new(-3 * tickSide,0,0),
                    Vector3.new(0,0,3 * tickSide),
                    Vector3.new(0,0,-3 * tickSide),
                    Vector3.new(0,3,0),
                    Vector3.new(0,-3,0),
                    Vector3.new(1.5,-3.2,1.5),
                    Vector3.new(-1.5,-3.2,-1.5)

                }

                for _,off in ipairs(offsets) do

                    if not running or seated then break end

                    hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(base + off, base)

                    task.wait(0.035)

                end

                tickSide = -tickSide

            end

        end)

    end
})



TrollTab:AddButton({
    Name = "Kill Ônibus",
    Callback = function()

        if not selectedPlayer then return end

        local target = Players:FindFirstChild(selectedPlayer)
        if not target or not target.Character then return end

        local character = plr.Character
        if not character then return end

        local humanoid = character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
        local hrp = character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")

        if not humanoid or not hrp then return end

        local targetHumanoid = target.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
        local targetHRP = target.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")

        if not targetHumanoid or not targetHRP then return end

        -- IR SPAWN VEICULOS
        hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(1181.83,76.08,-1158.83)

        task.wait(0.3)

        -- LIMPAR VEICULOS
        pcall(function()
            ReplicatedStorage.RE["1Ca1r"]:FireServer("DeleteAllVehicles")
        end)

        -- SPAWN BUS
        pcall(function()
            ReplicatedStorage.RE["1Ca1r"]:FireServer("PickingCar","SchoolBus")
        end)

        -- ESPERAR BUS
        local bus
        repeat
            task.wait()
            bus = Workspace.Vehicles:FindFirstChild(plr.Name.."Car")
        until bus

        -- POSIÇÃO DO SEAT
        hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(1171.46,84.27,-1166.66)

        task.wait(0.5)

        local seat = bus:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("VehicleSeat") or bus:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("Seat")

        if seat then
            seat:Sit(humanoid)
        end

        -- ESPERAR VOCÊ SENTAR
        repeat task.wait() until humanoid.Sit

        local running = true
        local seated = false

        local sitConn
        sitConn = targetHumanoid.Seated:Connect(function(active)

            if active then

                seated = true
                running = false

                sitConn:Disconnect()

                -- TELEPORTAR PARA -400
                hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(hrp.Position.X,-400,hrp.Position.Z)

                -- FAZER PULAR
                humanoid.Jump = true

                -- ESPERAR CAIR ATÉ -450
                task.spawn(function()

                    while hrp.Position.Y > -450 do
                        task.wait()
                    end

                    -- TELEPORTAR PARA SPAWN VEICULOS
                    hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(1181.83,76.08,-1158.83)

                end)

            end

        end)

        task.spawn(function()

            local tickSide = 1

            while running and not seated do

                if not target.Character then break end

                local base = targetHRP.Position

                local offsets = {

                    Vector3.new(3 * tickSide,0,0),
                    Vector3.new(-3 * tickSide,0,0),
                    Vector3.new(0,0,3 * tickSide),
                    Vector3.new(0,0,-3 * tickSide),

                    Vector3.new(0,3,0),
                    Vector3.new(0,-3,0),

                    Vector3.new(1.5,-3.2,1.5),
                    Vector3.new(-1.5,-3.2,-1.5)

                }

                for _,off in ipairs(offsets) do

                    if not running or seated then break end

                    hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(base + off, base)

                    task.wait(0.035)

                end

                tickSide = -tickSide

            end

        end)

    end
})



TrollTab:AddButton({
    Name = "Kill Boat",
    Callback = function()

        if not selectedPlayer then return end

        local Players = game:GetService("Players")
        local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")

        if not targetHumanoid or not targetHRP then return end

        -- TELEPORTAR PARA SPAWN DO BARCO
        hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(1761.91,-4.00,69.07) * CFrame.Angles(0,math.rad(-6.93),0)

        local running = true

            if active then

                running = false
                seated = true

                sitConn:Disconnect()

                -- TELEPORTAR PARA -400
                hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(hrp.Position.X,-400,hrp.Position.Z)

                humanoid.Jump = true

                task.spawn(function()

                    while hrp.Position.Y > -450 do
                        task.wait()
                    end

                    -- VOLTAR SPAWN VEICULOS
                    hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(1181.83,76.08,-1158.83)

                end)

            end

        end)

        task.spawn(function()

            local tickSide = 1

            while running and not seated do

                if not target.Character then break end

                local base = targetHRP.Position

                local offsets = {

                    Vector3.new(3 * tickSide,0,0),
                    Vector3.new(-3 * tickSide,0,0),

                    Vector3.new(0,0,3 * tickSide),
                    Vector3.new(0,0,-3 * tickSide),

                    Vector3.new(0,3,0),
                    Vector3.new(0,-3,0),

                    Vector3.new(1.5,-3.2,1.5),
                    Vector3.new(-1.5,-3.2,-1.5)

                }

                for _,off in ipairs(offsets) do

                    if not running or seated then break end

                    hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(base + off, base)

                    task.wait(0.035)

                end

                tickSide = -tickSide

            end

        end)

    end
})





TrollTab:AddSection({"fling sofa"})

local Players = game:GetService("Players")
local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
local LocalPlayer = Players.LocalPlayer
local cam = workspace.CurrentCamera

local flingCrochActive = false

---------------------------------------------------
-- FUNÇÃO QUE FAZ O FLING
---------------------------------------------------

local function doFlingSofa()

    if not selectedPlayer then return end

    local target = Players:FindFirstChild(selectedPlayer)
    if not target or not target.Character then return end

    local char = LocalPlayer.Character
    if not char then return end

    local root = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
    local hum = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")

    local tRoot = target.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
    local tHum = target.Character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")

    if not (root and hum and tRoot and tHum) then return end

    -- CLEAR TOOLS
    local clearRemote = ReplicatedStorage.RE:FindFirstChild("1Clea1rTool1s")
    if clearRemote then
        clearRemote:FireServer("ClearAllTools")
    end

    task.wait(0.3)

    -- PEGAR SOFÁ
    local toolRemote = ReplicatedStorage.RE:FindFirstChild("1Too1l")
    if toolRemote then
        toolRemote:InvokeServer("PickingTools","Couch")
    end

    local original = root.CFrame

    local tool = LocalPlayer.Backpack:FindFirstChildOfClass("Tool")
    if tool then
        tool.Parent = char
    end

    workspace.FallenPartsDestroyHeight = -math.huge

    local bv = Instance.new("BodyVelocity")
    bv.Name = "FlingForce"
    bv.Velocity = Vector3.new(9e8,9e8,9e8)
    bv.MaxForce = Vector3.new(math.huge,math.huge,math.huge)
    bv.Parent = root

    hum:SetStateEnabled(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Seated,false)
    hum.PlatformStand = false

    cam.CameraSubject = tRoot

    local angle = 0
    local t = tick()

    while tick() - t < 3
    and target
    and target.Character
    and target.Character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid") do

        tRoot = target.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
        if not tRoot then break end

        angle += 30

        root.CFrame =
            CFrame.new(tRoot.Position + Vector3.new(0,1,0))
            * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(angle),0,0)

        root.Velocity = Vector3.new(9e8,9e8,9e8)
        root.RotVelocity = Vector3.new(9e8,9e8,9e8)

        task.wait()

    end

    bv:Destroy()

    hum:SetStateEnabled(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Seated,true)
    hum.PlatformStand = false

    root.CFrame = original

    cam.CameraSubject = hum

    for _,p in pairs(char:GetDescendants()) do
        if p:IsA("BasePart") then
            p.Velocity = Vector3.zero
            p.RotVelocity = Vector3.zero
        end
    end

    hum:UnequipTools()

    if toolRemote then
        toolRemote:InvokeServer("PickingTools","Couch")
    end

end

---------------------------------------------------
-- TOGGLE LOOP
---------------------------------------------------

        flingCrochActive = state

        if state then
            task.spawn(function()

                while flingCrochActive do
                    doFlingSofa()
                    task.wait(0.5)
                end

            end)
        end

    end
})

TrollTab:AddSection({"click"})

TrollTab:AddButton({
Name = "Click Fling Doors",
Description = "Clique em um jogador para flingar ele usando portas",
Callback = function()

local Players = game:GetService("Players")
local Workspace = game:GetService("Workspace")
local RunService = game:GetService("RunService")

local LocalPlayer = Players.LocalPlayer
local Character = LocalPlayer.Character or LocalPlayer.CharacterAdded:Wait()
local HRP = Character:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart")

local function isDoor(name)
name = string.lower(name)
return name:find("door") or name:find("doors") or name:find("porta")
end

-- BLACKHOLE
local BlackHole = Instance.new("Part")
BlackHole.Size = Vector3.new(100000,100000,100000)
BlackHole.Transparency = 1
BlackHole.Anchored = true
BlackHole.CanCollide = false
BlackHole.Name = "BlackHoleTarget"
BlackHole.Parent = Workspace

local baseAttachment = Instance.new("Attachment")
baseAttachment.Name = "BlackHoleAttachment"
baseAttachment.Parent = BlackHole

RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
if HRP then
BlackHole.CFrame = HRP.CFrame
end
end)

-- LISTA DE PORTAS
local ControlledDoors = {}

-- NETWORK POWER
if not getgenv().Network then

getgenv().Network = {
BaseParts = {},
Velocity = Vector3.new(15,15,15)
}

Network.RetainPart = function(part)
if typeof(part) == "Instance"
and part:IsA("BasePart")
and part:IsDescendantOf(Workspace) then

table.insert(Network.BaseParts,part)
part.CustomPhysicalProperties = PhysicalProperties.new(0,0,0,0,0)
part.CanCollide = false

end
end

RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()

pcall(function()
sethiddenproperty(LocalPlayer,"SimulationRadius",math.huge)
end)

for _,part in pairs(Network.BaseParts) do
if part:IsDescendantOf(Workspace) then
part.Velocity = Network.Velocity
end
end

end)

end

-- PREPARAR PORTA
local function SetupPart(part)

if not part:IsA("BasePart") or part.Anchored or not isDoor(part.Name) then return end
if part:FindFirstChild("DoorAttached") then return end

part.CanCollide = false
Network.RetainPart(part)

for _,obj in ipairs(part:GetChildren()) do
if obj:IsA("AlignPosition") or obj:IsA("Torque") or obj:IsA("Attachment") then
obj:Destroy()
end
end

local marker = Instance.new("BoolValue")
marker.Name = "DoorAttached"
marker.Parent = part

local a1 = Instance.new("Attachment")
a1.Parent = part

local align = Instance.new("AlignPosition")
align.Parent = part
align.Attachment0 = a1
align.Attachment1 = baseAttachment
align.MaxForce = 1e20
align.MaxVelocity = math.huge
align.Responsiveness = 99999

local torque = Instance.new("Torque")
torque.Parent = part
torque.Attachment0 = a1
torque.RelativeTo = Enum.ActuatorRelativeTo.World
torque.Torque = Vector3.new(
math.random(-10e5,10e5)*90000,
math.random(-10e5,10e5)*90000,
math.random(-10e5,10e5)*90000
)

table.insert(ControlledDoors,{Part=part,Align=align})

end

-- DETECTAR PORTAS EXISTENTES
for _,obj in ipairs(Workspace:GetDescendants()) do
if obj:IsA("BasePart") and isDoor(obj.Name) then
SetupPart(obj)
end
end

-- NOVAS PORTAS
Workspace.DescendantAdded:Connect(function(obj)
if obj:IsA("BasePart") and isDoor(obj.Name) then
SetupPart(obj)
end
end)

-- PUXAR PORTAS
RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()

if HRP then

for _,part in pairs(Network.BaseParts) do
if part and part.Parent and isDoor(part.Name) then
part.Velocity = (HRP.Position - part.Position) * 60
end
end

end

end)

-- TOOL
local tool = Instance.new("Tool")
tool.Name = "Fling Porta"
tool.RequiresHandle = false
tool.Parent = LocalPlayer.Backpack

tool.Activated:Connect(function()

local mouse = LocalPlayer:GetMouse()
local target = mouse.Target
if not target then return end

local player = Players:GetPlayerFromCharacter(target:FindFirstAncestorOfClass("Model"))
if not player or player == LocalPlayer then return end

local char = player.Character
if not char then return end

local targetHRP = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
if not targetHRP then return end

local targetAttachment = targetHRP:FindFirstChild("DoorTarget")

if not targetAttachment then
targetAttachment = Instance.new("Attachment")
targetAttachment.Name = "DoorTarget"
targetAttachment.Parent = targetHRP
end

for _,data in ipairs(ControlledDoors) do
if data.Align then
data.Align.Attachment1 = targetAttachment
end
end

task.wait(5)

for _,data in ipairs(ControlledDoors) do
if data.Align then
data.Align.Attachment1 = baseAttachment
end
end

end)

end
})




TrollTab:AddSection({"Orbit TROLL"})

local Players = game:GetService("Players")
local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")

OrbitSettings = {
Speed = 5,
Distance = 6,
Height = 0,
Fling = false,
Stick = false,
Crazy = false
}

--------------------------------------------------
-- SLIDERS
--------------------------------------------------

TrollTab:AddSlider({
Name = "Orbit Speed",
Min = 1,
Max = 100,
Default = 5,
Callback = function(v)
OrbitSettings.Speed = v
end
})

TrollTab:AddSlider({
Name = "Distance",
Min = 0,
Max = 20,
Default = 6,
Callback = function(v)
OrbitSettings.Distance = v
end
})

TrollTab:AddSlider({
Name = "Height",
Min = -10,
Max = 10,
Default = 0,
Callback = function(v)
OrbitSettings.Height = v
end
})

--------------------------------------------------
-- MODES
--------------------------------------------------

TrollTab:AddToggle({
Name = "Fling Ball",
Default = false,
Callback = function(v)
OrbitSettings.Fling = v
end
})

TrollTab:AddToggle({
Name = "Stick Ball",
Default = false,
Callback = function(v)
OrbitSettings.Stick = v
end
})

TrollTab:AddToggle({
Name = "Crazy Ball",
Default = false,
Callback = function(v)
OrbitSettings.Crazy = v
end
})

--------------------------------------------------
-- ORBIT FUNCTION
--------------------------------------------------

function orbitBall(targetChar,modeName)

if not targetChar or not targetChar:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then return end

local player = Players.LocalPlayer
local char = player.Character or player.CharacterAdded:Wait()
local backpack = player:WaitForChild("Backpack")

local ballsFolder = workspace:WaitForChild("WorkspaceCom"):WaitForChild("001_SoccerBalls")

--------------------------------------------------
-- PEGAR BOLA
--------------------------------------------------

if not backpack:FindFirstChild("SoccerBall") and not char:FindFirstChild("SoccerBall") then

ReplicatedStorage.RE["1Too1l"]:InvokeServer("PickingTools","SoccerBall")

end

repeat task.wait()
until backpack:FindFirstChild("SoccerBall") or char:FindFirstChild("SoccerBall")

local tool = backpack:FindFirstChild("SoccerBall")

if tool then
tool.Parent = char
end

repeat task.wait()
until ballsFolder:FindFirstChild("Soccer"..player.Name)

local orb = ballsFolder:FindFirstChild("Soccer"..player.Name)

if not orb then return end

orb.Name = modeName
orb.CanCollide = false
orb.Massless = true
orb.CustomPhysicalProperties = PhysicalProperties.new(0.0001,0,0)

--------------------------------------------------
-- FLING POWER
--------------------------------------------------

if orb:FindFirstChild("FlingPower") then
orb.FlingPower:Destroy()
end

if OrbitSettings.Fling then

local bv = Instance.new("BodyVelocity")
bv.Name = "FlingPower"
bv.Velocity = Vector3.new(9e8,9e8,9e8)
bv.MaxForce = Vector3.new(math.huge,math.huge,math.huge)
bv.P = 9e9
bv.Parent = orb

end

--------------------------------------------------
-- LOOP
--------------------------------------------------

local loop = Instance.new("BoolValue")
loop.Name = modeName.."Loop"
loop.Parent = char

task.spawn(function()

while loop.Parent and orb and orb.Parent and targetChar and targetChar.Parent do

local hrp = targetChar:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")

if not hrp then break end

local angle = tick() * OrbitSettings.Speed

--------------------------------------------------
-- STICK MODE
--------------------------------------------------

if OrbitSettings.Stick then

orb.CFrame = hrp.CFrame * CFrame.new(0,0,-2)

--------------------------------------------------
-- CRAZY MODE
--------------------------------------------------

elseif OrbitSettings.Crazy then

local randomOffset = Vector3.new(
math.random(-6,6),
math.random(-4,4),
math.random(-6,6)
)

orb.CFrame = hrp.CFrame + randomOffset

--------------------------------------------------
-- ORBIT NORMAL
--------------------------------------------------

else

local offset = CFrame.new(
math.cos(angle)*OrbitSettings.Distance,
OrbitSettings.Height,
math.sin(angle)*OrbitSettings.Distance
)

orb.CFrame = hrp.CFrame * offset

end

task.wait(1/120)

end

end)

end

--------------------------------------------------
-- TOGGLES
--------------------------------------------------

TrollTab:AddToggle({
Name = "Orbit Ball (Self)",
Default = false,
Callback = function(state)

local char = Players.LocalPlayer.Character
local loop = char and char:FindFirstChild("OrbitSelfLoop")

if state then
orbitBall(char,"OrbitSelf")
elseif loop then
loop:Destroy()
end

end
})

TrollTab:AddToggle({
Name = "Orbit Ball",
Default = false,
Callback = function(state)

local target = selectedPlayer and Players:FindFirstChild(selectedPlayer)

if not target then return end

local char = Players.LocalPlayer.Character
local loop = char and char:FindFirstChild("OrbitTargetLoop")

if state then
orbitBall(target.Character,"OrbitTarget")
elseif loop then
loop:Destroy()
end

end
})




TrollTab:AddSection({"Placas"})

local Players = game:GetService("Players")

local textoPlaca = ""

    Name = "Texto da Placa",
    PlaceholderText = "Digite o texto",
    Callback = function(v)
        textoPlaca = v
    end
})

--------------------------------------------------
-- FUNÇÃO TROCAR PLACA
--------------------------------------------------

local function trocarPlacaPlayer(player, txt)

    if player
    and player.Character
    and player.Character:FindFirstChild("Sign") then

        player.Character.Sign.ToolSound:FireServer(
            "Sign",
            "SignWords",
            txt
        )

    end

end

--------------------------------------------------
-- BOTÃO ALL
--------------------------------------------------

TrollTab:AddButton({
    Name = "Trocar Placa ALL",
    Callback = function()

        for _,plr in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
            trocarPlacaPlayer(plr,textoPlaca)
        end

    end
})

--------------------------------------------------
-- BOTÃO PLAYER
--------------------------------------------------

TrollTab:AddButton({
    Name = "Trocar Placa Player",
    Callback = function()

        if selectedPlayer then

            local target = Players:FindFirstChild(selectedPlayer)

            if target then
                trocarPlacaPlayer(target,textoPlaca)
            end

        end

    end
})

--------------------------------------------------
-- LOOP ALL
--------------------------------------------------

TrollTab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Loop Placa ALL",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(state)

        loopAll = state

        if state then

            task.spawn(function()

                while loopAll do

                    for _,plr in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
                        trocarPlacaPlayer(plr,textoPlaca)
                    end

                    task.wait(0.5)

                end

            end)

        end

    end
})

--------------------------------------------------
-- LOOP PLAYER
--------------------------------------------------

TrollTab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Loop Placa Player",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(state)

        loopTarget = state

        if state then

            task.spawn(function()

                while loopTarget do

                    if selectedPlayer then

                        local target = Players:FindFirstChild(selectedPlayer)

                        if target then
                            trocarPlacaPlayer(target,textoPlaca)
                        end

                    end

                    task.wait(0.5)

                end

            end)

        end

    end
})




TrollTab:AddSection({"anti tools"})

-- SERVICES
local Players = game:GetService("Players")
local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
local LocalPlayer = Players.LocalPlayer

-- VARIÁVEIS
local antiAll = false

--------------------------------------------------
-- FUNÇÃO REMOVER TOOL
--------------------------------------------------

local function removeTools(target)

    if target
    and target.Character then

        local tool = target.Character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Tool")

        if tool then

            local triggerRemote = ReplicatedStorage.RE:FindFirstChild("1Playe1rTrigge1rEven1t")
            local clearRemote = ReplicatedStorage.RE:FindFirstChild("1Clea1rTool1s")

            if triggerRemote and clearRemote then

                local args1 = {
                    [1] = "AcceptedToolToServer",
                    [2] = tool.Name,
                    [3] = target
                }

                triggerRemote:FireServer(unpack(args1))

                local args2 = {
                    [1] = "ClearAllTools"
                }

                clearRemote:FireServer(unpack(args2))

            end

        end

    end

end

--------------------------------------------------
-- ANTI TOOLS ALL (LOOP)
--------------------------------------------------

TrollTab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Anti Tools ALL",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(v)

        antiAll = v

        if v then

            task.spawn(function()

                while antiAll do

                    for _,player in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
                        if player ~= LocalPlayer then
                            removeTools(player)
                        end
                    end

                    task.wait(0.01)

                end

            end)

        end

    end
})

--------------------------------------------------
-- ROUBAR TOOLS ALL (1 VEZ)
--------------------------------------------------

TrollTab:AddButton({
    Name = "Roubar Tools ALL (1x)",
    Callback = function()

        for _,player in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
            if player ~= LocalPlayer then
                removeTools(player)
            end
        end

    end
})


TrollTab:AddSection({"+18"})

local Players = game:GetService("Players")
local RunService = game:GetService("RunService")
local plr = Players.LocalPlayer

--------------------------------------------------
-- VARIÁVEIS
--------------------------------------------------

local moveSpeed = 5
local speed = 10

local enabledFrontBack = false
local enabledGoGo = false

local connectionFront
local connectionGo

--------------------------------------------------
-- SLIDER VELOCIDADE FRENTE/TRÁS
--------------------------------------------------

TrollTab:AddSlider({
    Name = "velocidade de frente e trás +18",
    Min = 1,
    Max = 100,
    Default = 5,
    Increment = 1,
    Callback = function(v)
        moveSpeed = v
    end
})

--------------------------------------------------
-- TOGGLE TELEPORT FRENTE/TRÁS
--------------------------------------------------

TrollTab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Teleport Troll (On / Off)",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(state)

        enabledFrontBack = state

        if connectionFront then
            connectionFront:Disconnect()
            connectionFront = nil
        end

        if not state or not selectedPlayer then return end

        local timeOffset = 0

        connectionFront = RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function(dt)

            if not enabledFrontBack then return end

            local target = Players:FindFirstChild(selectedPlayer)
            if not target or not target.Character then return end

            local thrp = target.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")

            local char = plr.Character
            local hrp = char and char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")

            if not (thrp and hrp) then return end

            timeOffset += dt * (moveSpeed * 0.3)

            local baseDistance = 4.5
            local oscillation = math.sin(timeOffset) * 3

            local verticalOffset = math.sin(timeOffset * 2) * 0.6

            local targetPos =
                thrp.Position
                - thrp.CFrame.LookVector * (baseDistance + oscillation)
                + Vector3.new(0, verticalOffset, 0)

            local shake = Vector3.new(
                math.random(-10,10) / 70,
                math.random(-10,10) / 70,
                0
            )

            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.lookAt(
                targetPos + shake,
                thrp.Position
            )

        end)

    end
})

--------------------------------------------------
-- SLIDER VELOCIDADE GOGOGO
--------------------------------------------------

TrollTab:AddSlider({
    Name = "Velocidade do gogogogo",
    Min = 1,
    Max = 100,
    Default = 10,
    Increment = 1,
    Callback = function(v)
        speed = v
    end
})

--------------------------------------------------
-- TOGGLE GOGOGO PLAYER
--------------------------------------------------

TrollTab:AddToggle({
    Name = "gogogogo no player +18",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(state)

        enabledGoGo = state

        if connectionGo then
            connectionGo:Disconnect()
            connectionGo = nil
        end

        if not state or not selectedPlayer then return end

        local timeValue = 0

        connectionGo = RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function(dt)

            if not enabledGoGo then return end

            local target = Players:FindFirstChild(selectedPlayer)
            if not target or not target.Character then return end

            local tChar = target.Character
            local tRoot = tChar:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
            local tHead = tChar:FindFirstChild("Head")

            local char = plr.Character
            local hrp = char and char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")

            if not (tRoot and tHead and hrp) then return end

            local myHipHeight = hrp.Size.Y * 0.5

            local heightOffset = Vector3.new(
                0,
                tHead.Size.Y * 0.4 + myHipHeight * 0.15,
                0
            )

            timeValue += dt * speed

            local backAndForth = math.sin(timeValue) * 2.5

            local finalPosition =
                tRoot.Position
                + tRoot.CFrame.LookVector * (3 + backAndForth)
                + heightOffset

            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.lookAt(finalPosition, tHead.Position)

        end)

    end
})





--////////////////////////////////////////////////////
--// SKYBOX TAB
local skyboxTab = Window:MakeTab({
    Title = "Skybox e Nuke",
    Icon = "rbxassetid://7733746980"
})

-- SERVICES
local Players = game:GetService("Players")
local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")

local LocalPlayer = Players.LocalPlayer
local Character = LocalPlayer.Character or LocalPlayer.CharacterAdded:Wait()
local humanoid = Character:WaitForChild("Humanoid")

--====================================================
-- CONTROLES

local NukeActive = false
local SkyboxActive = false

local NukeTracks = {}
local SkyboxTracks = {}

local NukeSavedBody = {}
local SkyboxSavedBody = {}

local RestoreExecuted = false

----------------------------------------------------
-- PARAR ANIMAÇÕES
----------------------------------------------------

local function stopTracks(tbl)

    for _,t in pairs(tbl) do
        pcall(function()
            t:Stop()
            t:Destroy()
        end)
    end

    for k in pairs(tbl) do
        tbl[k] = nil
    end

end

----------------------------------------------------
-- SALVAR BODY
----------------------------------------------------

local function saveBody(store)

    local d = humanoid:GetAppliedDescription()

    store[1] = d.Torso
    store[2] = d.RightArm
    store[3] = d.LeftArm
    store[4] = d.RightLeg
    store[5] = d.LeftLeg
    store[6] = d.Head

end

----------------------------------------------------
-- RESTAURAR BODY
----------------------------------------------------

local function restoreBody(store)

    if #store > 0 then

        pcall(function()
            ReplicatedStorage.Remotes.ChangeCharacterBody:InvokeServer(store)
        end)

        for k in pairs(store) do
            store[k] = nil
        end

    end

end

----------------------------------------------------
-- RESTORE FINAL
----------------------------------------------------

local function executeFinalRestore()

    if RestoreExecuted then return end
    RestoreExecuted = true

    local args = {
        {
            376532000,
            376531012,
            376530220,
            376531703,
            376531300,
            0
        }
    }

    pcall(function()
        ReplicatedStorage.Remotes.ChangeCharacterBody:InvokeServer(unpack(args))
    end)

end

--====================================================
-- N U K E

skyboxTab:AddSection({"Nuke"})

skyboxTab:AddToggle({

    Name = "Nuke",
    Default = false,

    Callback = function(value)

        if value then

            RestoreExecuted = false

            if SkyboxActive then
                SkyboxActive = false
                stopTracks(SkyboxTracks)
                restoreBody(SkyboxSavedBody)
            end

            NukeActive = true

            saveBody(NukeSavedBody)

            task.wait(0.2)

            pcall(function()
                ReplicatedStorage.Remotes.ChangeCharacterBody:InvokeServer({
                    123402086843885,
                    100839513065432,
                    78300682916056,
                    86276701020724,
                    78409653958165,
                    15093053680
                })
            end)

            task.wait(0.3)

            local a1 = Instance.new("Animation")
            a1.AnimationId = "rbxassetid://70883871260184"

            local t1 = humanoid:LoadAnimation(a1)
            t1.Priority = Enum.AnimationPriority.Action4
            t1:Play(0.1,1,0.01)

            table.insert(NukeTracks,t1)

            task.wait(0.4)

            local a2 = Instance.new("Animation")
            a2.AnimationId = "rbxassetid://3695333486"

            local t2 = humanoid:LoadAnimation(a2)
            t2.Priority = Enum.AnimationPriority.Movement
            t2:Play()

            table.insert(NukeTracks,t2)

        else

            NukeActive = false

            stopTracks(NukeTracks)
            restoreBody(NukeSavedBody)

            if not NukeActive and not SkyboxActive then
                executeFinalRestore()
            end

        end

    end
})

--====================================================
-- N U K E FLASH

skyboxTab:AddToggle({

    Name = "Nuke FlashBack",
    Default = false,

    Callback = function(value)

        if not value then return end

        stopTracks(NukeTracks)

        local anim = Instance.new("Animation")
        anim.AnimationId = "rbxassetid://70883871260184"

        local track = humanoid:LoadAnimation(anim)

        track:Play()
        track:AdjustSpeed(5)

        table.insert(NukeTracks,track)

    end

})


--====================================================
-- CONTROLES

skyboxTab:AddToggle({

    Name = "Skybox",
    Default = false,

    Callback = function(value)

        if value then

            RestoreExecuted = false

            if NukeActive then
                NukeActive = false
                stopTracks(NukeTracks)
                restoreBody(NukeSavedBody)
            end

            SkyboxActive = true

            saveBody(SkyboxSavedBody)

            task.wait(0.2)

            pcall(function()
                ReplicatedStorage.Remotes.ChangeCharacterBody:InvokeServer({
                    100839513065432,
                    nil,nil,nil,nil,nil
                })
            end)

            task.wait(0.3)

            local a1 = Instance.new("Animation")
            a1.AnimationId = "rbxassetid://70883871260184"

            local t1 = humanoid:LoadAnimation(a1)
            t1.Priority = Enum.AnimationPriority.Action4
            t1:Play(0.1,1,0.01)

            table.insert(SkyboxTracks,t1)

            task.wait(0.4)

            local a2 = Instance.new("Animation")
            a2.AnimationId = "rbxassetid://369533346"

            local t2 = humanoid:LoadAnimation(a2)
            t2.Priority = Enum.AnimationPriority.Movement
            t2:Play()

            table.insert(SkyboxTracks,t2)

        else

            SkyboxActive = false

            stopTracks(SkyboxTracks)
            restoreBody(SkyboxSavedBody)

            if not NukeActive and not SkyboxActive then
                executeFinalRestore()
            end

        end

    end
})

-- BOTÃO TRANSPARENTE

skyboxTab:AddButton({
    Name = "Transparente",
    Callback = function()

        local Players = game:GetService("Players")
        local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")

        local player = Players.LocalPlayer
        local character = player.Character or player.CharacterAdded:Wait()

        local SHIRT_ID = "rbxassetid://8911599186"
        local PANTS_ID = "rbxassetid://17475390991"

        local shirt = character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Shirt")
        local pants = character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Pants")

        local currentShirt = shirt and shirt.ShirtTemplate or ""
        local currentPants = pants and pants.PantsTemplate or ""

        local hasOurShirt = currentShirt == SHIRT_ID
        local hasOurPants = currentPants == PANTS_ID

        if hasOurPants and not hasOurShirt then

            ReplicatedStorage.Remotes.WearShirt:InvokeServer(8911599186)

        elseif hasOurShirt and not hasOurPants then

            ReplicatedStorage.Remotes.WearPants:InvokeServer(17475390991)

        elseif not hasOurShirt and not hasOurPants then

            ReplicatedStorage.Remotes.WearPants:InvokeServer(17475390991)
            ReplicatedStorage.Remotes.WearShirt:InvokeServer(8911599186)

        else

            warn("Já está com a roupa transparente completa")

        end

    end
})

-- RGB CORPO

local rgbAtivo = false
local rgbThread

local cores = {
"Light reddish violet","Salmon","Sunrise","Carnation pink","Pink","Hot pink",
"Really red","Tawny","Burgundy","Maroon","Cocoa","Rust","CGA brown","Beige",
"Brick yellow","Burlap","Fawn brown","Br. yellowish orange","Olive","New Yeller",
"Br. yellowish green","Mint","Artichoke","Lime green","Grime","Forest green",
"Parsley green","Earth green","Slime green","Toothpaste","Pastel light blue",
"Cyan","Bright blue","Really blue","Dark blue","Navy blue","Royal purple",
"Magenta","Bright violet","Eggplant","Mulberry","Institutional white",
"Mid gray","Cloudy grey","Flint","Fossil","Medium stone grey",
"Dark stone grey","Smoky grey","Black","Really black","Dirt brown",
"Pine Cone","Brown","Dark nougat","Light orange","Pastel brown"
}

local function iniciarRGB()

    if rgbThread then return end

    rgbThread = task.spawn(function()

        while rgbAtivo do

            for _,cor in ipairs(cores) do

                if not rgbAtivo then break end

                pcall(function()
                    ReplicatedStorage.Remotes.ChangeBodyColor:FireServer(cor)
                end)

                task.wait(0.02)

            end

        end

        rgbThread = nil

    end)

end

skyboxTab:AddToggle({

    Name = "RGB Corpo",
    Default = false,

    Callback = function(v)

        rgbAtivo = v

        if v then
            iniciarRGB()
        end

    end

})



local CarTab = Window:MakeTab({
    Title = "Car",
    Icon = "rbxassetid://7733708835"
})

CarTab:AddSection({"Speed Car/Boat & Turbo"})

--==================================================
-- VALORES
--==================================================

local speedValue = 200
local turboValue = 11.3

--==================================================
-- FUNÇÕES
--==================================================

-- Carro
local function applyCarSpeed(vehicle)

    local seat = vehicle:FindFirstChild("Seats") and vehicle.Seats:FindFirstChild("VehicleSeat")
    if not seat then return end

    pcall(function()
        seat.MaxSpeed = speedValue
    end)

    for _, v in pairs(seat:GetChildren()) do
        if v:IsA("NumberValue") then
            v.Value = speedValue
        end
    end

end


local function applyCarTurbo(vehicle)

    local seat = vehicle:FindFirstChild("Seats") and vehicle.Seats:FindFirstChild("VehicleSeat")
    if not seat then return end

    pcall(function()
        seat.Turbo = turboValue
    end)

    for _, v in pairs(seat:GetChildren()) do
        if v:IsA("NumberValue") and v.Name:lower():find("turbo") then
            v.Value = turboValue
        end
    end

end


-- Barco
local function applyBoatSpeed(vehicle)

    local body = vehicle:FindFirstChild("Body")
    if not body then return end

    local seat = body:FindFirstChild("VehicleSeat")

    if seat then
        pcall(function()
            seat.MaxSpeed = speedValue
        end)
    end

    -- força valores internos
    for _, obj in pairs(body:GetDescendants()) do
        if obj:IsA("NumberValue") then
            obj.Value = speedValue
        end
    end

    -- fallback físico
    if vehicle.PrimaryPart then
        vehicle.PrimaryPart.AssemblyLinearVelocity =
            vehicle.PrimaryPart.CFrame.LookVector * speedValue
    end

end


--==================================================
-- APPLY GERAL
--==================================================

local function applySpeedAll()

    local folder = workspace:FindFirstChild("Vehicles")
    if not folder then return end

    local count = 0

    for _, v in pairs(folder:GetChildren()) do
        if v:FindFirstChild("Seats") then
            applyCarSpeed(v)
            count += 1
        elseif v:FindFirstChild("Body") then
            applyBoatSpeed(v)
            count += 1
        end
    end

    print("Speed aplicado em:", count, "veículos")

end


local function applyTurboAll()

    local folder = workspace:FindFirstChild("Vehicles")
    if not folder then return end

    local count = 0

    for _, v in pairs(folder:GetChildren()) do
        if v:FindFirstChild("Seats") then
            applyCarTurbo(v)
            count += 1
        end
    end

    print("Turbo aplicado em:", count, "carros")

end


--==================================================
-- UI
--==================================================

CarTab:AddTextBox({
    Name = "Speed",
    PlaceholderText = "200",
    Callback = function(v)
        local n = tonumber(v)
        if n then speedValue = n end
    end
})

CarTab:AddTextBox({
    Name = "Turbo",
    PlaceholderText = "11.3",
    Callback = function(v)
        local n = tonumber(v)
        if n then turboValue = n end
    end
})

CarTab:AddButton({
    Name = "Aplicar Speed",
    Callback = function()
        applySpeedAll()
    end
})

CarTab:AddButton({
    Name = "Aplicar Turbo",
    Callback = function()
        applyTurboAll()
    end
})

print("Speed Car / Speed Boat Forçado | Turbo Car OK")

local Players = game:GetService("Players")
local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
local Remotes = ReplicatedStorage:WaitForChild("Remotes")
local plr = Players.LocalPlayer

-- CRIAR ABA
local SkinsTab = Window:MakeTab({
    Title = "Skins",
    Icon = "rbxassetid://105837152438777"
})

SkinsTab:AddSection({"Copy avatar"})

-- ===============================
-- DROPDOWN (MESMO SISTEMA DO TROLL)
-- ===============================

local selectedSkinPlayer = nil
local skinDropdown

local function getPlayersSkins()
    local t = {}
    for _, p in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
        if p ~= plr then
            table.insert(t, p.Name)
        end
    end
    return t
end

skinDropdown = SkinsTab:AddDropdown({
    Name = "Escolher Player",
    Options = {},
    Callback = function(v)
        selectedSkinPlayer = v
    end
})

local function refreshSkinDropdown()
    local players = getPlayersSkins()
    skinDropdown:Set(players)

    if selectedSkinPlayer and not Players:FindFirstChild(selectedSkinPlayer) then
        selectedSkinPlayer = nil
        skinDropdown:Set("")
    end
end

refreshSkinDropdown()

SkinsTab:AddButton({
    Name = "Atualizar Lista",
    Callback = refreshSkinDropdown
})

-- ===============================
-- BOTÃO COPY AVATAR
-- ===============================

SkinsTab:AddButton({
    Name = "Copiar Avatar",
    Callback = function()

        if not selectedSkinPlayer then return end

        local LP = Players.LocalPlayer
        local LChar = LP.Character
        local TPlayer = Players:FindFirstChild(selectedSkinPlayer)

        if not (LChar and TPlayer and TPlayer.Character) then return end

        local LHumanoid = LChar:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
        local THumanoid = TPlayer.Character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
        if not (LHumanoid and THumanoid) then return end

        -- RESET TOTAL DO LOCALPLAYER
        local LDesc = LHumanoid:GetAppliedDescription()

        -- REMOVER ACESSÓRIOS
        for _, acc in ipairs(LDesc:GetAccessories(true)) do
            if acc.AssetId and tonumber(acc.AssetId) then
                Remotes.Wear:InvokeServer(tonumber(acc.AssetId))
                task.wait(0.2)
            end
        end

        -- REMOVER ROUPAS
        if tonumber(LDesc.Shirt) then
            Remotes.Wear:InvokeServer(tonumber(LDesc.Shirt))
            task.wait(0.2)
        end

        if tonumber(LDesc.Pants) then
            Remotes.Wear:InvokeServer(tonumber(LDesc.Pants))
            task.wait(0.2)
        end

        -- REMOVER FACE
        if tonumber(LDesc.Face) then
            Remotes.Wear:InvokeServer(tonumber(LDesc.Face))
            task.wait(0.2)
        end

        -- COPIAR DO PLAYER ALVO
        local PDesc = THumanoid:GetAppliedDescription()

        -- PARTES DO CORPO
        local argsBody = {
            [1] = {
                [1] = PDesc.Torso,
                [2] = PDesc.RightArm,
                [3] = PDesc.LeftArm,
                [4] = PDesc.RightLeg,
                [5] = PDesc.LeftLeg,
                [6] = PDesc.Head
            }
        }

        Remotes.ChangeCharacterBody:InvokeServer(unpack(argsBody))
        task.wait(0.5)

        -- ROUPAS
        if tonumber(PDesc.Shirt) then
            Remotes.Wear:InvokeServer(tonumber(PDesc.Shirt))
            task.wait(0.3)
        end

        if tonumber(PDesc.Pants) then
            Remotes.Wear:InvokeServer(tonumber(PDesc.Pants))
            task.wait(0.3)
        end

        -- FACE
        if tonumber(PDesc.Face) then
            Remotes.Wear:InvokeServer(tonumber(PDesc.Face))
            task.wait(0.3)
        end

        -- ACESSÓRIOS
        for _, v in ipairs(PDesc:GetAccessories(true)) do
            if v.AssetId and tonumber(v.AssetId) then
                Remotes.Wear:InvokeServer(tonumber(v.AssetId))
                task.wait(0.3)
            end
        end

        -- COR DO CORPO
        local SkinColor = TPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Body Colors")
        if SkinColor then
            Remotes.ChangeBodyColor:FireServer(tostring(SkinColor.HeadColor))
            task.wait(0.3)
        end

        -- ANIMAÇÃO IDLE
        if tonumber(PDesc.IdleAnimation) then
            Remotes.Wear:InvokeServer(tonumber(PDesc.IdleAnimation))
            task.wait(0.3)
        end

    end
})




SkinsTab:AddSection({"Trocar Pernas"})

--==================================================
-- FUNÇÃO BASE (NÃO MEXER)
--==================================================
local function ApplyLeg(rightLegId, leftLegId)

    local player = Players.LocalPlayer
    local humanoid = player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
    if not humanoid then return end

    local desc = humanoid:GetAppliedDescription()

    Remotes.ChangeCharacterBody:InvokeServer({
        desc.Torso,
        desc.RightArm,
        desc.LeftArm,
        rightLegId or desc.RightLeg,
        leftLegId or desc.LeftLeg,
        0
    })

end

    Name = "Escolher Perna",
    Options = LegNames,
    Callback = function(selectedName)

        for _, leg in ipairs(LEGS) do
            if leg.name == selectedName then

                if leg.type == "Right" then
                    ApplyLeg(leg.id, nil)

                elseif leg.type == "Left" then
                    ApplyLeg(nil, leg.id)

                end

                break
            end
        end

    end
})

--==================================================
-- FUNÇÃO BASE
--==================================================
local function CreateEffectDropdown(title, effectTable)

    local options = {}

    for _, effect in ipairs(effectTable) do
        table.insert(options, effect.name)
    end

    SkinsTab:AddDropdown({
        Name = title,
        Options = options,
        Callback = function(selected)

            for _, effect in ipairs(effectTable) do
                if effect.name == selected then
                    ApplyEmmiter:InvokeServer(effect.id, effect.code)
                    break
                end
            end

        end
    })

end

--==================================================
-- CRIAR DROPDOWN AUTOMÁTICO
--==================================================
local function CreateBodyDropdown(categoryName, bodyTable)

    local options = {}

    for _, body in ipairs(bodyTable) do
        table.insert(options, body.name)
    end

    SkinsTab:AddDropdown({
        Name = categoryName,
        Options = options,
        Callback = function(selected)

            for _, body in ipairs(bodyTable) do
                if body.name == selected then
                    ApplyBody(body.ids)
                    break
                end
            end

        end
    })

end

--==================================================

    CreateBodyDropdown(categoryName, bodyTable)
end

--==================================================
-- FUNÇÃO PARA CRIAR DROPDOWN AUTOMÁTICO
--==================================================
local function CriarDropdownItem(nomeCategoria, tabelaItens)

    local opcoes = {}

    for _, item in ipairs(tabelaItens) do
        table.insert(opcoes, item.nome)
    end

    SkinsTab:AddDropdown({
        Name = nomeCategoria,
        Options = opcoes,
        Callback = function(selecionado)

            for _, item in ipairs(tabelaItens) do
                if item.nome == selecionado then

                    pcall(function()
                        Remotes.Wear:InvokeServer(item.id)
                    end)

                    break
                end
            end

        end
    })

end

--==================================================
-- GERAR TODOS AUTOMATICAMENTE
--==================================================
for categoria, tabelaItens in pairs(Itens) do
    CriarDropdownItem(categoria, tabelaItens)
end





--==================================================
-- GERAR TODOS AUTOMATICAMENTE
--==================================================
for categoria, tabelaItens in pairs(Itens) do
    CriarDropdownItem(categoria, tabelaItens)
end

    Title = "ITENS ALL",
    Icon = "rbxassetid://11860859170"
})

--////////////////////////////////////////////////////
--// SERVIÇOS
local Players = game:GetService("Players")
local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
local plr = Players.LocalPlayer

--////////////////////////////////////////////////////
--// REMOTE
local RemoteEvent =
    ReplicatedStorage
        :WaitForChild("RE")
        :WaitForChild("1Playe1rTrigge1rEven1t")

--////////////////////////////////////////////////////
--// FUNÇÃO PEGAR TOOL
local function GiveTool(toolName)

    if not toolName then return end

    local args = {
        [1] = "AcceptedToolToServer",
        [2] = toolName,
        [3] = plr
    }

    RemoteEvent:FireServer(unpack(args))

end

--////////////////////////////////////////////////////
--// FUNÇÃO CRIAR DROPDOWN
local function CreateDropdown(title, itemTable)

    local names = {}

    for name,_ in pairs(itemTable) do
        table.insert(names, name)
    end

    ItemTab:AddDropdown({
        Name = title,
        Options = names,
        CurrentOption = "",
        Callback = function(selected)

            local toolName = itemTable[selected]

            if toolName then
                GiveTool(toolName)
            end

        end
    })

end

--// ===============================

--// ===============================
local rgbSpeed = 3

RGBTab:AddSlider({
    Name = "Velocidade RGB",
    Description = "Aumenta a velocidade do efeito RGB",
    Min = 1,
    Max = 10,
    Increase = 1,
    Default = 3,
    Callback = function(Value)
        rgbSpeed = Value
    end
})

--// ===============================
--// FUNÇÕES
--// ===============================
local function getRainbowColor(speedMultiplier)
    local h = (tick() * speedMultiplier % 10) / 10
    return Color3.fromHSV(h, 1, 1)
end

local function fireServer(eventName, args)
    local RE = ReplicatedStorage:FindFirstChild("RE")
    if RE and RE:FindFirstChild(eventName) then
        pcall(function()
            RE[eventName]:FireServer(unpack(args))
        end)
    end
end

--// ===============================
--// SEÇÃO NOME / BIO
--// ===============================
RGBTab:AddSection({ "RGB para usar em você" })

local nameBioRGBActive = false
RGBTab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Nome + Bio RGB",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(state)
        nameBioRGBActive = state
        if state then
            task.spawn(function()
                while nameBioRGBActive do
                    local color = getRainbowColor(rgbSpeed)

                    fireServer("1RPNam1eColo1r", { "PickingRPNameColor", color })
                    fireServer("1RPNam1eColo1r", { "PickingRPBioColor", color })

                    task.wait(0.03)
                end
            end)
        end
    end
})

--// CONTROLE
local rgbAtivo = false
local rgbThread

--// LISTA DE CORES
local cores = {
    "Light reddish violet","Salmon","Sunrise","Carnation pink","Pink","Hot pink",
    "Really red","Tawny","Burgundy","Maroon","Cocoa","Rust","CGA brown","Beige",
    "Brick yellow","Burlap","Fawn brown","Br. yellowish orange","Olive","New Yeller",
    "Br. yellowish green","Mint","Artichoke","Lime green","Grime","Forest green",
    "Parsley green","Earth green","Slime green","Toothpaste","Pastel light blue",
    "Cyan","Bright blue","Really blue","Dark blue","Navy blue","Royal purple",
    "Magenta","Bright violet","Eggplant","Mulberry","Institutional white",
    "Mid gray","Cloudy grey","Flint","Fossil","Medium stone grey",
    "Dark stone grey","Smoky grey","Black","Really black","Dirt brown",
    "Pine Cone","Brown","Dark nougat","Light orange","Pastel brown"
}

--// LOOP RGB
local function iniciarRGB()

    if rgbThread then return end

    rgbThread = task.spawn(function()

        while rgbAtivo do

            for _, cor in ipairs(cores) do

                if not rgbAtivo then break end

                pcall(function()
                    ReplicatedStorage.Remotes.ChangeBodyColor:FireServer(cor)
                end)

                task.wait(0.02) -- EXTREMAMENTE RÁPIDO

            end

        end

        rgbThread = nil

    end)

end

--// TOGGLE RGB
RGBTab:AddToggle({
    Name = "RGB Corpo",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(v)

        rgbAtivo = v

        if v then
            iniciarRGB()
        end

    end
})

RGBTab:AddSection({ "Itens / Tools" })

local radioRGBActive = false

RGBTab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Rádio RGB",
    Description = "RGB contínuo no rádio",
    Default = false,

    Callback = function(state)

        radioRGBActive = state

        if state then

            task.spawn(function()

                while radioRGBActive do

                    local color = getRainbowColor(rgbSpeed)

                    local success, remote = pcall(function()
                        return LocalPlayer.PlayerGui.ToolGui.ToolSettings.Settings.PropsColor.SetColor
                    end)

                    if success and remote then
                        remote:FireServer(color)
                    end

                    task.wait(0.03)

                end

            end)

        end

    end
})


local function toolRGB(toggleVar)

    task.spawn(function()

        while getgenv()[toggleVar] do

            local color = getRainbowColor(rgbSpeed)

            local gui = LocalPlayer:FindFirstChild("PlayerGui")

            if gui and gui:FindFirstChild("ToolGui") then

                local props = gui.ToolGui.ToolSettings.Settings.PropsColor

                if props and props:FindFirstChild("SetColor") then

                    pcall(function()
                        props.SetColor:FireServer(color)
                    end)

                end

            end

            task.wait(0.1)

        end

    end)

end


RGBTab:AddToggle({
    Name = "RGB Megafone",
    Default = false,

    Callback = function(Value)

        getgenv().rgbMegafone = Value
        toolRGB("rgbMegafone")

    end
})


RGBTab:AddToggle({
    Name = "RGB Rosquinha",
    Default = false,

    Callback = function(Value)

        getgenv().rgbRosquinha = Value
        toolRGB("rgbRosquinha")

    end
})
