--// RP NAME + BIO TYPE & DELETE (SEM BUG DE SPEED)

local RPTextRemote = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
    :WaitForChild("RE")
    :WaitForChild("1RPNam1eTex1t")

local RPNameText = ""
local RPBioText = ""

local RPNameEnabled = false
local RPBioEnabled = false

local NameSpeed = 30
local BioSpeed = 30

local function getDelay(speed)
    speed = math.clamp(speed, 1, 60)
    return 0.02 + (60 - speed) * 0.003
end

-- ================= RP NAME =================

RGBTab:AddTextBox({
    Name = "RP Name Texto",
    Placeholder = "Digite o RP Name",
    Callback = function(v)
        RPNameText = v
    end
})

RGBTab:AddSlider({
    Name = "Velocidade RP Name",
    Min = 1,
    Max = 60,
    Default = 30,
    Callback = function(v)
        NameSpeed = v
    end
})

RGBTab:AddToggle({
    Name = "RP Name ON / OFF",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(state)

        RPNameEnabled = state

        if not state or RPNameText == "" then return end

        task.spawn(function()

            while RPNameEnabled do

                -- ESCREVER
                for i = 1, #RPNameText do

                    if not RPNameEnabled then return end

                    RPTextRemote:FireServer(
                        "RolePlayName",
                        string.sub(RPNameText, 1, i)
                    )

                    task.wait(getDelay(NameSpeed))

                end

                task.wait(0.4)

                -- APAGAR (DE TRÁS PRA FRENTE)
                for i = #RPNameText - 1, 0, -1 do

                    if not RPNameEnabled then return end

                    RPTextRemote:FireServer(
                        "RolePlayName",
                        string.sub(RPNameText, 1, i)
                    )

                    task.wait(getDelay(NameSpeed))

                end

                task.wait(0.4)

            end

        end)

    end
})


-- ================= RP BIO =================

RGBTab:AddTextBox({
    Name = "RP Bio Texto",
    Placeholder = "Digite o RP Bio",
    Callback = function(v)
        RPBioText = v
    end
})

RGBTab:AddSlider({
    Name = "Velocidade RP Bio",
    Min = 1,
    Max = 60,
    Default = 30,
    Callback = function(v)
        BioSpeed = v
    end
})

RGBTab:AddToggle({
    Name = "RP Bio ON / OFF",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(state)

        RPBioEnabled = state

        if not state or RPBioText == "" then return end

        task.spawn(function()

            while RPBioEnabled do

                -- ESCREVER
                for i = 1, #RPBioText do

                    if not RPBioEnabled then return end

                    RPTextRemote:FireServer(
                        "RolePlayBio",
                        string.sub(RPBioText, 1, i)
                    )

                    task.wait(getDelay(BioSpeed))

                end

                task.wait(0.4)

                -- APAGAR
                for i = #RPBioText - 1, 0, -1 do

                    if not RPBioEnabled then return end

                    RPTextRemote:FireServer(
                        "RolePlayBio",
                        string.sub(RPBioText, 1, i)
                    )

                    task.wait(getDelay(BioSpeed))

                end

                task.wait(0.4)

            end

        end)

    end
})

    Default = SelectedName,
    Callback = function(v)
        SelectedName = v
    end
})

--////////////////////////////////////////////////////
--// FUNÇÃO SOM LOCAL
local function PlayLocalSound(id)
    local sound = Instance.new("Sound")
    sound.SoundId = "rbxassetid://" .. tostring(id)
    sound.Volume = 1
    sound.Looped = false
    sound.Parent = SoundService
    sound:Play()

    task.delay(10, function()
        if sound then
            sound:Destroy()
        end
    end)
end

--////////////////////////////////////////////////////
--// FUNÇÃO EXECUTAR SOM + GUN
local function ExecuteSoundGun(id)
    id = tostring(id)

    PlayLocalSound(id)
    SoundRemote:FireServer(workspace, id, 1)

    task.wait(0.05)

    for _, plr in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
        if plr.Character and plr.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
            local hrp = plr.Character.HumanoidRootPart

            local gunArgs = {
                hrp,
                hrp,
                Vector3.new(0, -1, 0),
                Vector3.new(0, 0, 0),
                hrp,
                hrp,
                id,
                id,
                { true },
                {
                    25,
                    Vector3.new(0.25, 0.25, 100),
                    BrickColor.new(24),
                    0.25,
                    Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic,
                    0.25
                },
                true,
                false
            }

            GunRemote:FireServer(unpack(gunArgs))
        end
    end
end

    Name = "🔫 TOCAR SOM SELECIONADO 😈",
    Callback = function()
        local id = SoundIDs[SelectedName]
        if id then
            ExecuteSoundGun(id)
        end
    end
})

local RunService = game:GetService("RunService")

LoopSpeed = LoopSpeed or 1
LoopEnabled = false

--////////////////////////////////////////////////////
--// SLIDER 1 ATÉ 350
SoundGunTab:AddSlider({
    Name = "⚡ Velocidade do Loop",
    Min = 1,
    Max = 350,
    Default = LoopSpeed,
    Increment = 1,
    ValueName = "x",
    Callback = function(v)
        LoopSpeed = v
    end
})

--////////////////////////////////////////////////////
--// LOOP FUNCIONAL REAL
SoundGunTab:AddToggle({
    Name = "⬆ LOOP SOM DA LISTA",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(state)
        LoopEnabled = state

        if state then
            task.spawn(function()
                while LoopEnabled do
                    local id = SoundIDs[SelectedName]
                    if id then
                        ExecuteSoundGun(id)
                    end

                    -- Delay inteligente
                    local waitTime
                    if LoopSpeed <= 1 then
                        waitTime = 2
                    else
                        waitTime = math.clamp(2 / LoopSpeed, 0.005, 2)
                    end

                    task.wait(waitTime)
                end
            end)
        end
    end
})

--==================================================
-- FUNÇÃO TOCAR MÚSICA
--==================================================
local function playMusic(id)
    local RE = ReplicatedStorage:FindFirstChild("RE")
    if not RE then return end
    id = tostring(id)

    pcall(function()
        RE.PlayerToolEvent:FireServer("ToolMusicText", id)
        RE["1Player1sHous1e"]:FireServer("PickHouseMusicText", id)
        RE["1Player1sCa1r"]:FireServer("VehicleMusicPlay", id)
        RE["1NoMoto1rVehicle1s"]:FireServer("PickingScooterMusicText", id)
    end)
end

--==================================================
-- DROPDOWN FUNCIONAL
--==================================================
local function makeDropdown(tab, name, data)
    local options = {}
    for k,_ in pairs(data) do
        table.insert(options, k)
    end

    tab:AddDropdown({
        Name = name,
        Options = options,
        Callback = function(Value)
            local id = data[Value]
            if id and id ~= "" then
                playMusic(id)
            end
        end
    })
end

makeDropdown(MusicTab, "Funk", Funk)
makeDropdown(MusicTab, "Phonk", Phonk)
makeDropdown(MusicTab, "Forró", Forro)
makeDropdown(MusicTab, "Aleatórios", Aleatorio)

--==================================================
-- BOTÃO PARAR MÚSICA
--==================================================
MusicTab:AddButton({
    Name = "Parar Música",
    Callback = function()
        playMusic("0")
    end
})

print("✔ Sistema de música carregado COMPLETO")



--==================================================
-- Seção aviso
--==================================================
MusicTab:AddSection({ "As músicas só estão pegando em caixa de som" })

--==================================================
-- ID PERSONALIZADO
--==================================================
MusicTab:AddSection({ "🎵 ID Personalizado (Escolha qualquer música)" })

local CustomMusicID = ""

-- Caixa de texto para digitar ID
MusicTab:AddTextBox({
    Name = "Digite o ID da Música",
    PlaceholderText = "Ex: 73778985963973",
    Callback = function(text)
        CustomMusicID = tostring(text)
    end
})

-- Botão para tocar ID digitado
MusicTab:AddButton({
    Name = "▶ TOCAR ID DIGITADO",
    Callback = function()
        if CustomMusicID ~= "" and CustomMusicID ~= nil then
            playMusic(CustomMusicID)
        end
    end
})
